 kaha jaataa he ki in donon dinon par jo log vrath karte hai or bhagwaan ganesh ji kaa samaran karte hai unke sabhi dukh dur ho jate hai

e
 wealth, knowledge, mastery, etc
, while Sankashti Chaturthi is done with the purpose of mitigating (eliminating) the obstacles of life

 unhone abhi tak har chunaav isi ko model dikhaakar vot maangen hai or chunaav jite hai
 After Gujarat, elections are also held in many other states
 jaise rajasthan, madhyapradesh, chhattisgarh, karnataka rajya main
 Many of these states have a BJP government
 bijepi agar gujarat main harati he to in par bhi asar padegaa
 Since the BJP is still moving ahead with Modi's face
 gujarat paar to bedaa paar!gauratlab he ki gujarat chunaav piem modi or bijepi adhyaksh amit shah kaa garh he
 Therefore, the biggest challenge for the BJP is to win the Gujarat elections
 isi tarah agar congress chunaav jitati he to rahul gandhi ke liye adhyaksh pad sanbhaalane ke baad shandaar shuruyaat hogi
 And as an opposition leader, there will be a big change in his image
 is chunaav ko 2019 kaa semifinal mana ja rahaa he
 Will have to see who will be the last bet
 madhya pradesh main police ne aatank failaane waalon par shikanja kasate hue simi ke 43 kaaryakartaaon ko andeh ke aadhaar par giraftaar kiya he
 State Chief Minister Shivraj Singh Chauhan gave this information on Friday
 aatankwaad ko vartmaan main desh or rajya kii sabase badi samasya bataate hue mukhyamantri chouhan ne kaha ki police ne ek bada abhiyaan chalaate hue puure rajya bhar se simi ke 43 kaaryakartaaon ko giraftaar kiya he
 Chief Minister Chauhan reached Katni amid heavy rains during his Jan Aashirvad Yatra
 is maukey par unhone ek party raily ko bhi sambodhit kiya
 The woman claimed that she met Kumar in Tis Hazari court
 usne mahila se phone par baat karne ko kaha
 When the woman called, she said that she should talk to a lawyer named Anshul
 shikayatakarta ne aarope lagaaya ki jab vah vakil se milane pahunchi to unhone bataaya ki kumaar ne mahila se 70,000 rupaye dene ko kaha he
 The woman approached the CBI on this
 baad main sibiai ne chapa maar kumaar or anshul ko rishwat lete pakad liya

 ) The membership campaign of Aam Aadmi Party (AAP) in Jharkhand has been mired in controversies as soon as it started
 pradesh ke lagbhag har bade shaharon main aap party ke ek se adhik karyaalay khul gaye hai or yahaan sabhi sadsy banane se lekar chanda ugaahi main lage hai
 These days, the road side office of the Aam Aadmi Party is visible at every major square-intersection of Ranchi
 koi baqayada offis kholkar baitha he to kaiyon ne road ke bagal main mej sajaakar sadsy bananaa shuru kar diya he
 None of these has been officially authorized by the party
 is sabake baavjood aap party kii topi lagaae ye sabhi sadsy banane ke saath-saath chanda ugaahi main bhi lage hai
 The interesting thing is that all the parties are also trying to justify themselves by citing the Constitution
 haalanki ab tak inamen se kisi ko bhi aadhikarik taur par kendriya cameti kii ore se manyata nahin mili he
 In such a situation, the entire membership campaign has come under suspicion
 gauratlab he ki aap party ne 10 se 26 janvari tak puure desh main ni:shulk sadsy banane kaa abhiyaan chalaa rakhaa he
 In this regard, AAP Party District Convenor Ajay Chaudhary said that its information has been given to the National Assembly
 vahiin party ke kaaryakarta es
 N
 singh ne kaha ki party samvidhan main likhaa he ki koi bhi karyaalay khol saktaa he
 In the Northern Command of the Army, the companies offering high prices, keeping the rules in mind, have been given the contract to supply frozen chicken without checking
 sena ke purv general javaanon ko frozen chiken khilaane ke sakht khilaaf hai or teen saansadon ne bhi is silsile main raksha mantri ko chitthee likhi he
 However, on this issue, the Army says that the entire process was completed before the contract and such allegations are being made due to wrong motives and mutual enmity of the vendors
 raksha mantralay ne pichley saal sena ke paanch cmand main frozen chiken supplai kaa ek payalat project shuru kiya jo ek saal ke liye tha lekin isi faisle kaa galat istemaal kar uttari cmand ke ladakh or kargil sector main bhi frozen chiken kii supplai shuru ho gai
 The Army has set different standards for supplying frozen chicken in such difficult areas, while the Northern Command recently struck a short-term agreement with Tamil Nadu-based company Suguna Foods in which the rules were shelved
 uttari cmand ne 15 november se 14 disambar tak ke liye chiken supplai ke liye tender mangaya lekin tender jamaa karne ke aakhri din baaki fermon ko kaha gaya ki ek maheene kaa tender radd ho gaya he
 In this case, no one has the answer as to how Suguna Foods got the contract
 suguna foods ke 117 rupee prati kilo ke tender ko manjuuri mili jabaki inhi sharto par pashchimi cmand ko duusare saplir sirf 96 rupee kii rate par chiken supplai kar rahe hai
 So the army lost about 28 lakh rupees in this contract
 kaayade se jis company ko theka diya jaataa he sena ke afasar uski jaanch karte hai lekin suguna foods ko jaanch se pehle hi frozen chiken supplai kii ijazat mil gai
 Suguna Foods has a factory in Tamil Nadu, which got the contract at a time when Kerala has banned chicken from Tamil Nadu due to the possibility of bird flu in Karnataka
 suguna foods 100 fisadi halaal chiken taiyaar karti he jabaki sena main majahab ko lekar behad ehtiyaat barti jaati he or 80 fisadi jhatka chiken istemaal hota he
 Lieutenant General Jaswal, who served as chief of the northern command, also says that the frozen chicken is not suitable for difficult areas like Ladakh and Kargil
 itnaa hi nahin, general jaswaal ke mutabik nijee companiyon ke haath supplai kii quality or rakrakhaav dekar sena baari galati kar rahi he
 a former General of the Western Command, chief, is also against giving frozen chicken to the soldiers instead of fresh chicken
 general hun siachin kii jang main hindustani fouz ke commander the or unka kahana he ki uttari cmand main sirf siachin main hi frozen chiken diya janaa chahie baaki ilaakon main nahin
 Three mps have also written a letter to Defense Minister AK Antony against the frozen chicken supply in the army
 tippaniyan Congress MP from Andhra Pradesh Sarva Satyanarayana considers the lobby of big companies behind this decision, while MP from Madhya Pradesh Gajendra Singh has raised the question of loss to the army
 bijepi saansad shahanwaaz hossain ne ise javaanon kii sehat ke liye nuksaandeh bataaya he
 In response to the letter of mps, the Defense Minister has assured to investigate the matter, but there is a question that who will guarantee the health of the soldiers who eat frozen chicken during this time

 Now Goa Chief Minister Manohar Parrikar is caught in a new controversy by calling all Indians as Hindus
 goa vidhansabha main buudhvaar ko unhone kaha ki kai videshi log sabhi bharatiyon ke liye 'hindu' shabd kaa istemaal karte hai or khadi deshon main to bharat ke musalmaan ko bhi hindu kaha jaataa he

 Parrikar said this while meditating on it
 hindu nahin, hindi kehalaate hai bhartiya!unki is baat par soshal media par kadi aapatti darj karai gai
 People wrote that Indians in Gulf countries are called 'hindi' and not 'hindus'
 parrikar kaa yah bayaan thodaa chaunkaane vaala he kyonki vah aam taur par vivaadon se dur rahete hai
 Parrikar, who studies at IIT Bombay, has an image of a development-oriented leader in the party

 lohanipur ilaake ke is parivaar kii kul sankhya 150 he
 This time, 8 people in this family will exercise their franchise for the first time
 lohanipur ilaake kaa chandel nivas ek parfect vot bank he, kyonki is parivaar ke 115 log voter hai
 The family of 150 lives in a multi-storey building at Chandel Niwas
 matadaataaon main 65 purush or 50 mahilaayein hai
 This time 8 new voters have also joined it, out of which 7 girls and 1 boy are included
 pehali baar vot dene vaali gitanjali or rashmi kaa utsaah dekhte hi banataa he

 'chhichhore' inhen do filmon kaa cocktail jaisi lagati he
 The story of 'chhichhore' gives a message to stay away from the mindset of not becoming a loser along with yari-friendship
 film main college ke din hai, yaari-dosti kaa majaa he, hostel life he or khel main sabakuch daanv par lagaana he

 yahi baat puraa majaa kirkira kar jaati he

 phir sushant singh bete ko thik karne ke liye apni lujar team kii kahani sunaate hai

 In a tweet, it is said that Dalit men are cowardly, only then people of Savarna society are raping Dalit daughters
 nishchit rup se internet jagat main maujuud dalit mahila adhikaar manch aisi baton kaa samarthan nahin karenge
 Fearing the cowardice of Dalit men means that the solution has been taken out in such a way that it will not happen if they are not cowardly
 zaahir he yah samasya kaa samaadhaan aisi lalakaaron se nahin nikalnaa he

 tippaniyan Whether or not Dalit thinkers and the organization's threat on Twitter can break the supremacy of the right wing present here, but their presence is telling that they are not going to remain silent without voicing their voice
 is ladaai ko kai log aarakshan samarthan or virodh kii dhaal se ladane lagate hai yaa iske naam par bachane lagate hai
 The issue of exploitation of Dalits is not just about reservation
 vaise yah jaanane main koi harz nahin ki dakshinpanthi takatein aarakshan ke alaava shoshan or daman ke in kisson par kya raay rakhti hai
 Ambedkar does not belong to anyone just by holding a rally in the name of Ambedkar on 14 April
 aaj na kal in sawaalon se takaraana hi hoga
 No public opinion can be modern or nationalist without solving these questions
 dalit muddon ko lekar bane in twitor handle par akhabaaron main chhapi un khabaron ko saajha kiya ja rahaa he jin par mukhyadhara kii media main koi charchaa nahin hoti, lekin hairaani kii baat he ki twitor kii duniya kaa bartaav mukhyadhara kii media se alag nahin he

 sankhya ke hisaab se do hazaar log bhi pholo nahin karte hai, lekin mudde yahaan bina kisi laag lapet ke uthaae gaye hai
